WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers payment processing when invoice package is complete
Triggers settlement hold if required proof is missing
Triggers factoring notice workflow if factor is listed
Triggers dispute workflow if invoice is disputed
Triggers aging alert if past due
Triggers billing exception review if flagged
Triggers command center alert if invoice is Held or Disputed

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers accessorial review workflow for unapproved charges
Triggers customer notification if unapproved charges exist
Triggers settlement hold if unapproved items remain unresolved
Triggers invoice attachment when summary is complete
Triggers threshold alert if total accessorials exceed review threshold
Triggers command center alert if threshold exceeded or unapproved items unresolved
BackOfficeFleet (BOF) — Billing and Settlement Operations

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers lumper reimbursement on carrier settlement
Triggers over-budget review if lumper exceeds load tender budget
Triggers settlement hold if receipt is missing or invalid
Triggers invoice and accessorial summary attachment when validated
Triggers command center alert if over-budget and unapproved

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers detention / layover charge on invoice
Triggers customer notification and approval workflow
Triggers dispute handling if customer contests
Triggers escalation if customer dispute remains unresolved
Triggers settlement hold if documentation incomplete
Triggers command center alert if dispute is open at invoice time

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers payment redirection to factoring company for all applicable invoices
Triggers Carrier-Broker Agreement Summary update
Triggers customer acknowledgment tracking
Triggers reminder follow-up if acknowledgment not received by follow-up date
Triggers escalation if acknowledgment overdue
Triggers settlement hold if payment routing is not confirmed
Triggers command center alert if acknowledgment is not received within deadline

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers payment hold in settlement system
Triggers carrier and customer notification
Triggers auto-escalation if hold exceeds defined timeframe
Triggers command center watch status
Triggers payment release workflow when all items resolved
Triggers partial payment if authorized
Triggers priority-based escalation timing (Standard / Urgent / Critical)
BackOfficeFleet (BOF) — Billing and Settlement Operations

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers payment processing when packet is Complete
Triggers settlement hold creation if packet is Incomplete
Triggers factoring payment routing if factor is listed
Triggers partial payment if authorized
Triggers past due escalation if aging exceeds threshold
Triggers command center alert if packet is On Hold or Under Review past due date
Triggers billing release per Rate Confirmation and Service Schedule requirements
SIGNATURES

WHAT DOES THIS DOCUMENT TRIGGER IN BOF?
Triggers lumper exception review workflow
Triggers supervisor approval workflow for additional amount
Triggers accessorial summary update
Triggers billing packet update
Triggers settlement hold if unresolved
Triggers claims / command center review if tied to cargo damage
Triggers customer notification if over-budget or exception-related
